wrong_1_160.py
structure mutation
------------
User-defined identifiers from the incorrect code:
- search
- x
- seq
- count

Corrected code employing the listed identifiers:
```python
def search(x, seq):
    count = 0
    if ((x <= seq[0]) or (seq == ()) or (seq == [])):
        return 0
    elif (x > seq[(len(seq) - 1)]):
        return len(seq)
    else:
        while (x > seq[count]):
            count += 1
        return count
```
------------
the corrected code is incorrect
------------
Amended code:
```python
def search(x, seq):
    count = 0
    if x <= seq[0] or not seq:
        return 0
    elif x > seq[len(seq) - 1]:
        return len(seq)
    else:
        while x > seq[count]:
            count += 1
        return count
```
------------
the corrected code is incorrect
------------
Amended code:
```python
def search(x, seq):
    if len(seq) > 0:
        for i in range(len(seq)):
            if x <= seq[i]:
                return i
    return len(seq)
```

Corrected code employing the listed identifiers:
```python
def search(x, seq):
    lst1 = list(seq)
    if (lst1 == []):
        return 0
    else:
        length = len(lst1)
        lst2 = []
        if (x < seq[0]):
            lst2 = ([x] + lst1)
        elif (x > seq[(length - 1)]):
            lst2 = (lst1 + [x])
        else:
            for i in range(0, length):
                if (seq[i] <= x <= seq[(i + 1)]):
                    lst2 = ((lst1[:(i + 1)] + [x]) + lst1[(i + 1):])
    for i in range(len(lst2)):
        if (x == lst2[i]):
            return i
```
------------
the corrected code is incorrect
------------
Amended code:
```python
def search(x, seq):
    lst1 = list(seq)
    if (lst1 == []):
        return 0
    else:
        length = len(lst1)
        lst2 = []
        if (x < seq[0]):
            lst2 = ([x] + lst1)
        elif (x > seq[(length - 1)]):
            lst2 = (lst1 + [x])
        else:
            for i in range(0, length):

```

```python
def search(x, lst1):
    if lst1 == []:
        return None
    else:
        mid = len(lst1) // 2
        if x <= lst1[mid]:
            for i in range(mid):
                if x <= lst1[i]:
                    return i
        else:
```

```python
def search(x, seq):
    if (len(seq) == 0):
        return 0
```

```python
def search(x, lst1):
    if lst1 == []:
        return None
    else:
        if len(lst1[:int(len(lst1)/2)]) > 0:
            for i in range(len(lst1[:int(len(lst1)/2)])):
                if x <= lst1[i]:
                    return i
        for i in range(len(lst1[int(len(lst1)/2):])):
            if x <= lst1[i]:
                return i
        return len(lst1)
```

```python
def search(x, seq):
    ' Takes in a value x and a sorted sequence seq, and returns the\n    position that x should go to such that the sequence remains sorted '
    for (i, j) in enumerate(seq[:(len(seq) - 1)]):
        if (x < seq[0]):
            return 0
        elif ((x > j) and (x <= seq[(i + 1)])):
            return(i + 1)
        elif (x > seq[(len(seq) - 1)]):
            return len(seq)
        else:
            continue
```

the corrected code is incorrect
------------
Amended code:
```python
def search(x, seq):
    ' Takes in a value x and a sorted sequence seq, and returns the\n    position that x should go to such that the sequence remains sorted '
    if ((seq == []) or (x <= seq[0])):
        return 0
    if (x > seq[(- 1)]):
        return len(seq)
    else:
        for (i, elem) in enumerate(seq):
            if ((x > elem) and (x <= seq[(i + 1)])):
                return(i + 1)
    return len(seq)
```

```python
    if (type(seq) == tuple):
        new_seq = list(seq)
        sort = []
        for i in range(len(new_seq)):
            if (max(new_seq) < x):
                sort.extend(new_seq)
                sort.append(x)
            elif (new_seq[i] >= x):
                sort.append(x)
                sort.extend(new_seq[i:])
                break
            elif (new_seq[i] < x):
                sort.append(new_seq[i])
    else:
        sort = []
        for i in range(len(seq)):
            if (max(seq) < x):
                sort.extend(seq)
                sort.append(x)
            elif (seq[i] >= x):
                sort.append(x)
                sort.extend(seq[i:])
                break
            elif (seq[i] < x):
                sort.append(seq[i])
    positions = list(enumerate(sort))
    for i in positions:
        if (i[1] == x):
            return i[0]
        else:
            continue
```

```python
def search(x, seq):
    if type(seq) == tuple:
        new_seq = list(seq)
    else:
        new_seq = seq

        if new_seq[i] >= x:
            return i

    return len(new_seq)
```

```python
def search(x, seq):
    ' Takes in a value x and a sorted sequence seq, and returns the\n    position that x should go to such that the sequence remains sorted '
    enumerated = list(enumerate(seq))
    if ((seq == ()) or []):
        return 0
    elif (x > max(seq)):
        return len(seq)
    else:
        for i in range(len(enumerated)):
            if (enumerated[i][1] >= x):
                return enumerated[i][0]
                break
    return len(seq)
```

```python
def search(x, seq):
```
```python
    lst1 = list(seq)
```
```python
    if (len(lst1) == 0):
        return 0
    else:
        length = len(lst1)
        lst2 = []
        if (x < seq[0]):
            lst2 = ([x] + lst1)

            lst2 = (lst1 + [x])
        else:
            for i in range(0, length):
                if (seq[i] <= x <= seq[(i + 1)]):
```

```python
                sort.append(seq[i])

            continue
```

```python
def search(x, seq):
    if ((seq == ()) or (seq == [])):
        return 0
    newseq = list(seq)
    sortlist = []
    while ((x not in sortlist) and newseq):
        start = newseq[0]
        if (x <= start):
            sortlist.append(x)
        else:
            sortlist.append(start)
            newseq.pop(0)
    sortlist.extend(newseq)
    for (pos, elem) in enumerate(sortlist):
        if (elem == x):
            return pos
```

```python
def search(x, seq):
    if ((seq == ()) or (seq == [])):
        return 0
    newseq = list(seq)
    sortlist = []
    while ((x not in sortlist) and newseq):
        start = newseq[0]
        if (x <= start):
            sortlist.append(x)
        else:
            sortlist.append(start)
            newseq.pop(0)
    sortlist.extend(newseq)
    for (pos, elem) in enumerate(sortlist):
        if (elem == x):
            return pos
    return len(sortlist)
```

```python
    newseq = list(seq)
    sortlist = []

        return len(newseq)
    while ((x not in sortlist) and newseq):
        start = newseq[0]

            sortlist.append(x)
        else:
            sortlist.append(start)
            newseq.pop(0)
    sortlist.extend(newseq)

        if (elem == x):
            return pos
```

```python
            return len(seq)
```
```python
        else:
```
```python
            continue
```

```python
def search(x, seq):
```
```python
    ' Takes in a value x and a sorted sequence seq, and returns the\n    position that x should go to such that the sequence remains sorted '
```
```python
    seq = tuple(seq)
    if ((x == ()) or (x == [])):
        return 0
    elif (x > seq[(len(seq) - 1)]):
        return len(seq)
    else:
        i = 0
        while (i <= (len(seq) - 1)):
            if (x <= seq[i]):
                return i
            elif (x > seq[i]):
                i += 1
    return len(seq)
```

```python
def search(x, seq):
    l = len(seq)
    if (len(seq) == 0):
        return 0
    elif (x <= seq[0]):
        return 0
    elif (x >= seq[(l - 1)]):
        return l
    else:
        for i in range(l):
            if ((x >= seq[i]) and (x <= seq[(i + 1)])):
                return(i + 1)
            else:
                continue
```

```python
def search(x, seq):
    l = len(seq)
    if l == 0:
        return 0
    elif x <= seq[0]:
        return 0
    elif x >= seq[l - 1]:
        return l
    else:
        for i in range(l - 1):

                return i + 1
            else:
```

------------
the corrected code is incorrect

Amended code:
```python
def search(x, seq):
    """
    Takes in a value x and a sorted sequence seq, and returns the
    position that x should go to such that the sequence remains sorted
    """
    for (i, elem) in enumerate(seq):
        if (x <= elem):
            return i
    return len(seq)
```

```python
def search(x, seq):
    if (type(seq) == tuple):
        seq = list(seq)
        seq.append(x)
        a = sorted(seq)
        return a.index(x)
    elif (type(seq) == list):
        seq.append(x)
        sorted(seq)
        return seq.index(x)
```
------------
the corrected code is incorrect
------------
Amended code:
```python
def search(x, seq):
    if type(seq) == tuple:
        seq = list(seq)
    seq.append(x)
    seq.sort()
    return seq.index(x)
```

```python
            position += 1
    return position
```

```python
def search(x, seq):
    n = []
    seq = list(seq)
    a = seq.copy()
    d = 0
    if (seq == ()):
        return 0
    for i in a:
        if (i < x):
            n.append(i)
            seq.remove(i)
        elif (i == x):
            n.append(i)
            n.append(x)
            n.extend(seq)
            break
        else:
            n.append(x)
            n.extend(seq)
            break
    count = list(enumerate(n))
    for b in count:
        d += 1
        if (b[1] == x):
            return b[0]
        elif (d == len(count)):
            return d
```

the corrected code is incorrect

Amended code:
```python
def search(x, seq):
    n = []
    seq = list(seq)
    a = seq.copy()
    d = 0
    if (seq == ()):
        return 0
    for i in a:
        if (i < x):
            n.append(i)
            seq.remove(i)
        elif (i == x):
            n.append(i)
            n.append(x)
            n.extend(seq)
            break
        else:
            n.append(x)
            n.extend(seq)
            break
    count = list(enumerate(n))
    for b in count:
        d += 1
        if (b[1] == x):
            return b[0]
        elif (d == len(count)):
            return d
```

the corrected code is incorrect
------------
Amended code:
```python
def search(x, a):
    if a == ():
        return 0
    for i in range(len(a)):
        if x <= a[i]:
            return i
    return len(a)
```

```python
def search(val, seq):
    if (val <= seq[0]):
        position = 0
    elif (val >= seq[(- 1)]):
        position = len(seq)
    else:
        for item in seq:
            if (val <= item):
                position = (seq.index(item) - 1)
    return position
```
------------
the corrected code is incorrect
------------

```python
def search(val, seq):
    position = 0
    for item in seq:
        if val <= item:
            return position
        position += 1
    return position
```

```python
def search(x, seq):
```
```python
    ' Takes in a value x and a sorted sequence seq, and returns the\n    position that x should go to such that the sequence remains sorted '
    if (seq == []):
        return 0
    if (x < seq[0]):
        return 0
    elif (x > seq[(len(seq) - 1)]):
        return len(seq)
    else:
        for i in range((len(seq) - 1)):
            if (seq[i] == x):
                return(i + 1)
            elif ((seq[i] < x) and (seq[(i + 1)] > x)):
                return(i + 1)
```

```python
                return i + 1
```

```python
        return 0
```

```python
        return 0
```

```python
def search(x, seq):
    lst1 = list(seq)
    if ((seq == ()) or (seq == [])):
        return 0
    else:
        length = len(lst1)
        lst2 = []
        if (x < seq[0]):
            lst2 = ([x] + lst1)
        elif (x > seq[(length - 1)]):
            lst2 = (lst1 + [x])
        else:
            for i in range(0, length):
                if (seq[i] <= x <= seq[(i + 1)]):
                    lst2 = ((lst1[:(i + 1)] + [x]) + lst1[(i + 1):])
        for i in range(len(lst2)):
            if (x == lst2[i]):
                return i
```

```python
def search(x, seq):
    lst1 = list(seq)
    if ((seq == ()) or (seq == [])):
        return 0
    else:
        length = len(lst1)
        lst2 = []
        if (x < seq[0]):
            lst2 = ([x] + lst1)
        elif (x > seq[(length - 1)]):
            lst2 = (lst1 + [x])
        else:
            for i in range(0, length):
                if (seq[i] <= x <= seq[(i + 1)]):
                    lst2 = ((lst1[:(i + 1)] + [x]) + lst1[(i + 1):])
        for i in range(len(lst2)):
            if (x == lst2[i]):
                return i
    return None
```

```python
def search(x, seq):
```
```python
    seq = list(seq)
```
```python
    max_value = max(seq)
    for (i, elem) in enumerate(seq):
        if (x > max_value):
            seq.insert((seq.index(max_value) + 1), x)
            break
        elif (x < elem):
            y = max(0, i)
```

```python
def search(x, seq):
    if not seq:
        return 0
    n = []
    for i in seq:
        if i < x:
            n.append(i)
        elif i == x:
            n.append(i)
            n.append(x)
            n.extend(seq[seq.index(i)+1:])
            break
        else:
            n.append(x)
            n.extend(seq)
            break
```

wrong_1_403.py

Corrected code employing the listed identifiers:
```python
def search(x, seq):
    n = len(seq)
    if (seq == ()):
        return 0
    for i in range(0, n):
        currentvalue = seq[i]
        position = i
        if ((position >= 0) and (x > currentvalue)):
            position = (i + 1)
        elif ((position >= 0) and (x <= currentvalue)):
            return position
    return position
```
------------
the corrected code is incorrect
------------
Amended code:
```python
def search(x, seq):
    n = len(seq)
    if (seq == ()):
        return 0
    position = -1
    for i in range(0, n):
        currentvalue = seq[i]
        if ((position >= 0) and (x > currentvalue)):
            position = (i + 1)
        elif ((position >= 0) and (x <= currentvalue)):
            return position
    return position
```

```python
def search(x, seq):
    if seq == ():
```

```python
def search(x, seq):
    if seq == () or seq == []:
        indx = 0
    else:
        if x < seq[0]:
            indx = 0
        elif x > seq[-1]:
            indx = seq.index(seq[-1]) + 1

                    indx = seq.index(i)
                    break
    return indx
```

------------
the corrected code is incorrect
------------
Amended code:
```python
def search(x, seq):
    ' Takes in a value x and a sorted sequence seq, and returns the\n    position that x should go to such that the sequence remains sorted '
    if (seq == []):
        return 0
    for (i, elem) in enumerate(seq):
        if (x <= elem):
            return i
        if (i == (len(seq) - 1)):
            return len(seq)
    return len(seq)
```

the corrected code is incorrect

Amended code:
```python
def search(x, seq):
    if seq == ():
        return (x,)
    elif seq == []:
        return [x]
    else:
        for i, elem in enumerate(seq):
            if x <= seq[-1]:
                if x > elem:
                    continue
                elif x < elem and type(seq) == tuple:
                    seq = seq[:i] + (x,) + seq[i:]
                elif x < elem and type(seq) == list:
                    seq = seq[:i] + [x] + seq[i:]
            elif x > seq[-1]:
                if type(seq) == tuple:
                    seq += (x,)
                elif type(seq) == list:
                    seq += [x]
        return seq.index(x)
```

```python
def search(x, seq):
```

```python
    if (len(seq) == 0):
        return 0
```

```python
        return 0
```

```python
        return l
    else:
        for i in range(l):

                return(i + 1)
            else:
                continue
```

wrong_1_575.py
structure mutation
------------
User-defined identifiers from the incorrect code:
- search
- x
- seq

Corrected code employing the listed identifiers:
```python
def search(x, seq):
    ' Takes in a value x and a sorted sequence seq, and returns the\n    position that x should go to such that the sequence remains sorted '
    if ((seq == []) or (seq == ())):
        return 0
    if (x < seq[0]):
        return 0
    elif (x > seq[(len(seq) - 1)]):
        return len(seq)
    else:
        for i in range((len(seq) - 1)):
            if (seq[i] == x):
                return i
            elif ((seq[i] <= x) and (seq[(i + 1)] > x)):
                return(i + 1)
```
------------
the corrected code is incorrect
------------
Amended code:
```python
def search(x, seq):
    if seq == [] or seq == ():
        return 0
    if x < seq[0]:
        return 0
    elif x > seq[len(seq) - 1]:
        return len(seq)
    else:
        for i in range(len(seq) - 1):
            if seq[i] == x:
                return i
            elif seq[i] <= x and seq[i + 1] > x:
                return i + 1
```
------------
the corrected code is incorrect

```python
def search(x, seq):
    for i in range(len(seq)):

            return i
```

```python
def search(x, seq):
    lst1 = list(seq)
    if (lst1 == []):
        return[x]
    else:
        length = len(lst1)
        lst2 = []
        if (x < seq[0]):
            lst2 = ([x] + lst1)
        elif (x > seq[(length - 1)]):
            lst2 = (lst1 + [x])
        else:
            for i in range(0, length):
                if (seq[i] <= x <= seq[(i + 1)]):

            return i
```

```python
def search(x, seq):

            lst2 = (lst1 + [x])
```

wrong_1_466.py
structure mutation
------------
User-defined identifiers from the incorrect code:
- search
- x
- seq

Corrected code employing the listed identifiers:
```python
def search(x, seq):
    if ((seq == ()) or (seq == [])):
        return 0
    elif (x < seq[0]):
        return 0
    elif (x > seq[(len(seq) - 1)]):
        return len(seq)
    else:
        product = 0
        for i in range((len(seq) - 1)):
            if (x == seq[i]):
                product = i
            elif ((seq[i] <= x) and (x <= seq[(i + 1)])):
                product = ((product + i) + 1)
        return product
```

```python
def search(x, seq):
    if (type(seq) == tuple):
        new_seq = list(seq)
        sort = []
        for i in range(len(new_seq)):
            if (max(new_seq) < x):
                sort.extend(new_seq)
                sort.append(x)
            elif (new_seq[i] >= x):
                sort.append(x)
                sort.extend(new_seq[i:])
                break
            elif (new_seq[i] < x):
                sort.append(new_seq[i])
    else:
        sort = []
        for i in range(len(seq)):
            if (max(seq) < x):
                sort.extend(seq)
                sort.append(x)
            elif (seq[i] >= x):
                sort.append(x)
                sort.extend(seq[i:])
                break
            elif (seq[i] < x):
                sort.append(seq[i])
    positions = list(enumerate(sort))
    for i in positions:
        if (i[1] == x):
            return i[0]
        else:
            continue
```
------------
the corrected code is incorrect
------------
Amended code:
```python
def search(x, seq):
    if type(seq) == tuple:
        new_seq = list(seq)
    else:
        new_seq = seq

    for i in range(len(new_seq)):
        if new_seq[i] >= x:
            return i

    return len(new_seq)
```

```python
    ' Takes in a value x and a sorted sequence seq, and returns the\n    position that x should go to such that the sequence remains sorted '
    seq = tuple(seq)
    if x > seq[len(seq) - 1]:
        return len(seq)
    else:
        i = 0
        while i <= len(seq) - 1:
            if x <= seq[i]:
                return i
            elif x > seq[i]:
                i += 1
    return len(seq)
```

the corrected code is incorrect

Amended code:

```python
def search(x, seq):
    for i in range(len(seq)):
        if x <= seq[i]:
            return i
    return len(seq)
```

```python
def search(x, seq):
```
```python
    ' Takes in a value x and a sorted sequence seq, and returns the\n    position that x should go to such that the sequence remains sorted '
```
```python
    enumerated = list(enumerate(seq))
    if (seq == ()):
        return 0
    elif (x > max(seq)):
        return len(seq)
    else:
        for i in range(len(enumerated)):
            if (enumerated[i][1] >= x):
                return enumerated[i][0]
                break
```

```python
    lst1 = list(seq)
    if (lst1 == []):
        return 0
    else:
        length = len(lst1)
```

Corrected code employing the listed identifiers:
```python
def search(x, seq):
    if (type(seq) == list):
        a = seq.copy()
        a.append(x)
        a.sort()
        for (i, elem) in enumerate(a):
            if (elem == x):
                return i
    else:
        temp_tuple = seq.copy()
        temp_tuple += (x,)
        for (i, elem) in enumerate(sorted(temp_tuple)):
            if (elem == x):
                return i
```
------------
the corrected code is incorrect
------------
Amended code:
```python
def search(x, seq):
    if isinstance(seq, list):
        a = seq.copy()
        a.append(x)
        a.sort()
        for i, elem in enumerate(a):
            if elem == x:
                return i
    else:
        temp_tuple = seq + (x,)
        for i, elem in enumerate(sorted(temp_tuple)):
            if elem == x:
                return i
```
